<text>Dairy is a great place to play 9 holes. The course is well maintained, and the driving range is the best in the area. The large putting practice area is nice too.

The new golf carts they introduced recently are fancy, but limit where you can drive. If you venture off the cart path to track down your ball, it will limit the speed to nearly 0, making the carts more of a hassle than convenience.

As someone who works 9-5 during the week, its frustrating that the staff forces you off the course at 7PM sharp. I‚Äôve been on the 8th tee box at 6:45 and been told by staff that I have to leave. A frustrating experience, especially after paying $50 for me and my guest to play a quick round.

To make the experience more frustrating, is the fact that I‚Äôve never seen a Marshall regulating the speed of play. We got stuck behind a ‚ÄúSingle" that in fact had his wife and toddler with him. They were using their slot as golf lessons. Not a great group to follow when trying to complete 9 holes before the 7pm curfew.

Hopefully Dairy Creek‚Äôs management will act on the customer feedback and extend their operating hours. It would be great to utilize the extra hour and a half of sunlight that goes unused each day.</text>< Pictures>
[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMZkLmZ4mDD1iX1dNFkH8O_X6bEgoF1U-GrUSZd=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//Pictures>
<resp>{'time': 1595895230408, 'text': 'Mr. Hoover, thanks for the feedback, insight, and suggestions. In addition to gps, electronic scorecards, and messaging systems, the new golf cars have a technology to help us monitor the golf cars and assist in the golfer experience. Yes they do slow down in areas in the roughs where the terrain gets steep or bumpy. This is to provide a more smooth ride for the golfer and to protect the front suspension of the golf cars so that we can limit our expenses, therefore keepIng our green fees low. The cars do slow down to 8 mph in these areas vs the standard 12 mph. If golf cars enter green complexes or tee box areas then the cars do slow to 2 mph or completely stop in some circumstances. These are highly prized areas of golf real estate and golf car traffic can do significant damage to these areas. We are trying to discourage golf car traffic in these areas to provide the best playing conditions and value to our customers. This may add a few steps to your round and for that we ask your understanding for the greater benefit of everyone. Finally, our mission at Dairy Creek is to grow the game and attract new customers. We welcome families, young people, and ‚Äúnewbies‚Äù to to play our course. The golf course is a great place to teach the game especially at the end of the day when traffic is light. We do everything in our power to notify the golfers that we close at 7 pm. Our website, voice service, email blasts, and staff profess these hours of operation. The early closure is to protect our staff during these uncertain times and to get them home to their families at a reasonable hour. < review>
Once a premier 18 hole course, the track is now the most challenging 9-hole course on the Central Coast.  The course was reduced due to water woes, but the back 9 was kept, and is in great shape, featuring 3 par 3's, 3 par 4's and 3 par 5's in a a majestic natural setting.  The green fees are very reasonable, at $15  to walk (add $9 per rider for cart), and a replay is just $5 ($1 for county card holders) to walk, and the twilight rate after 4 is just $14.< /review>

The food here is delicious!!!

That should be the full review. Not enough? Ok here is what I tried:
Short Rib Grilled Cheese. My wife had that one and didn't wanna share it with me cuz it was too good.
Buffalo Chicken Sandwich. Perfect buffalo flavor, not too strong, and matched perfectly with the slaw. Also got some sweet potato fries with it and they're amazing. Perfect texture and sweetness.
Finished it off with the Cinnamon Crunch Milkshake. One of my favorite cereals as a dessert was perfect on a typical sunny SoCal day.

I wish there was one of these in North Orange County so I wouldn't have to drive all the way down to south county to get some.</Review>

Had to give this place a go before it closed. Massively sad to see such a quality mom and pop BBQ place leave the Turlock area. All the meat is wonderfully tender and flavorful even without the delicious rub that comes alongside it. The prices are understandably high, as the quantity of food you get for your purchase is filling for even two people. I highly recommend people patronize this place while it's still around.</review>

< Review>
AWESOME SANDWICH PLACE! Kind of a tucked away gem, didn't think Google maps was directing me correctly. Anyways, great sandwich place to have a bite, there affordable and have a HUGE menu and it's not just sandwiches either. They have burgers, burritos numerous different types of food. Don't let the name fool you not only sandwiches! Definitely worth a try, great prices considering the portions are generous and so are the owners. Can't say enough good things and there macaroni salad is fantastic. My wife doesn't even like macaroni salad but everytime we eat here she gets it as a side, sometimes even gets an extra side to take home. That says something right there! They also have a good potato salad/sides options and everything else you would expect at a good sandwich shop. You can also order ahead for pick up if in a hurry or anything else. Grab a togo menu when your there, bc it's extensive and you will always be able to find something new the next time you go, see if you can work through the whole menu sometime, lol. Anyways great little sandwich, lunch, early dinner gem tucked away. Worth the visit!<//Review>

< review>
Love Trader Joe's, Dollar Tree and Simply Greek etc etc... The businesses are fantastic.. However the parking lot is beyond a nightmare. I purposely stay away unless it's in off hours. Today I came with my 8 yr old daughter. On our way out we were almost run over by a man and his wife in a minivan desperate for a close spot. He was not paying attention. I felt the wind and vibration from his van and I was behind my cart. My daughter who was on the side of the cart, had she been turned straight instead of sideways looking at me would have been hit. This man didn't care, refused to apologize, insisted he'd been there a long time. I was so flabbergasted. Two horrible lessons for my daughter to learn, 1) driving irresponsibly is ok and 2) you don't need to take responsibility when you are wrong. They definitely at the very least need cameras here and preferably a police presence who will stop these Mario Andretti drivers. So sad my day out with my girl ended like this. It's just wrong!!!</review>
